Tangail ******************** On 09-07-2023, a mobile court was held under the leadership of the learned Executive Magistrate Mocha Sultana Razia at George Court area of тАЛтАЛTangail District. 3 shopkeepers (1000+500+500) were fined a total of Tk 2000 as per section 5(g) of the Smoking and Tobacco Control Act 2005 (Amended-2013) for the crime of advertising tobacco products in the mobile court. Besides, the shopkeepers in the vicinity are informed about the tobacco control laws. Tangail Sadar Upazila Sanitary Inspector Shaheda Begum, Tangail DC Office Peshkar Md. Mizanur Rahman Mizan and Tangail district police administration along with Natab Program Officer Md.
